 		content: url('data:image/svg+xml; utf8, <svg width="15" height="13" viewBox="0 0 15 13" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g fill="black" fill-rule="evenodd"><g transform="translate(7)"><rect transform="rotate(45 4 4)" y="3" width="8" height="2" rx="1"/><rect transform="rotate(-45 4 9)" y="8" width="8" height="2" rx="1"/></g><rect x=".5" y="5.5" width="14" height="2" rx="1"/></g></svg>');
 		position: relative;
 		top: 1px;
 	}

    <script>
     /* Detect if back-forward caching is used.
 	   This caused issues in Safari, where only the clicked subcat would stay visible after hitting back. */
 	window.addEventListener('unload', function () {});
 	window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
 		if (event.persisted) {
 			resetAllSubcatItems()
 		}
 	});
 
 
 	function onReady(method) {
 		if (window.jQuery) {
 			method();
 		} else {
 			setTimeout(function() { onReady(method) }, 50);
 		}
 	}
 
 	// Desktop only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (!isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 
 		var $nav = $('.tt-main-navigation-module');
 		var $cat = $('.tt-homepage__cat');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 		var $panels = $('.tt-panels');
 		var $logoImg = $nav.find('.tt-logo img');
 
 		$logoImg.get(0).onload = null; // Can be removed when TRIDUP-5616 is implemented.
 
 		$nav.hover(makeNavWhite, makeNavTransparent);
 		$sports.hover(makeDriveInactive, makeDriveActive);
 		$cards.children().on('click', function() {
 			$('html, body').animate(
 				{
 					scrollTop: window.innerHeight,
 					duration: 600,
 					easing: 'swing'
 				})
 		});
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
 
 		equalizeHeights($cards.find('.tt-homepage__card__body'));
 		makeNavTransparent();
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeMenuSticky(scroll);
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeMenuSticky(scroll) {
 			if (scroll > 80) {
 				makeNavWhite();
 			} else if (scroll <= 80) {
 				makeNavTransparent();
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var cardTitleHeight = 80;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var imgBottom = $cat.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = imgBottom + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - imgBottom});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeNavWhite() {
 			$nav.removeClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeNavTransparent() {
 			var isPanelOpen = $panels.hasClass('in');
 			var isScrolledDown = window.scrollY > 80;
 			if (isPanelOpen || isScrolledDown) { return; }
 
 			$nav.addClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveActive() {
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveInactive() {
 			$drive.addClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function equalizeHeights($elements) {
 			var maxHeight = 0;
 			$elements.each(function(i, el) { maxHeight = Math.max(el.clientHeight, maxHeight) } );
 
 			$elements.height(maxHeight);
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 		$(window).on('resize', onScroll);
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var menuHeight = 80;
 			var cardTitleHeight = 60;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var categoriesHeight = $drive.height() + $sports.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = categoriesHeight + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight - menuHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - categoriesHeight});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile and desktop
 	onReady(function() {
 		var time = 0.3;
 		var ease = Quad.easeOut;
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $sportsSubcats = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $driveSubcats = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $sportsSubcatItems = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $driveSubcatItems = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $sportsButton = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 		var $driveButton = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 
 		addEventListeners();
 
 		function addEventListeners() {
 			$sports.on('click', onClickSports);
 			$drive.on('click', onClickDrive);
 			$sportsSubcatItems.on('click', onClickSportsSubcatItem);
 			$driveSubcatItems.on('click', onClickDriveSubcatItem);
 		}
 
 		function onClickSports() {
 			if($sportsSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close drive
 			TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickDrive(e) {
 			if($driveSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close sports
 			TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickSportsSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$sportsSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function onClickDriveSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$driveSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function resetAllSubcatItems() {
 			TweenLite.set($sportsButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 	})
    </script>

 		font-size: 18px;
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="zh"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "微软雅黑體", "Microsoft YaHei", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ko"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Nanum Barun Gothic", "Malgun Gothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ja"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Hiragino Kaku Gothic Pro", "Meiryo", "Osaka", "MS PGothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	.tt-homepage__card__body {
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 		transition: height 200ms;
 	}

    <script>
     /* Detect if back-forward caching is used.
 	   This caused issues in Safari, where only the clicked subcat would stay visible after hitting back. */
 	window.addEventListener('unload', function () {});
 	window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
 		if (event.persisted) {
 			resetAllSubcatItems()
 		}
 	});
 
 
 	function onReady(method) {
 		if (window.jQuery) {
 			method();
 		} else {
 			setTimeout(function() { onReady(method) }, 50);
 		}
 	}
 
 	// Desktop only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (!isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 
 		var $nav = $('.tt-main-navigation-module');
 		var $cat = $('.tt-homepage__cat');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 		var $panels = $('.tt-panels');
 		var $logoImg = $nav.find('.tt-logo img');
 
 		$logoImg.get(0).onload = null; // Can be removed when TRIDUP-5616 is implemented.
 
 		$nav.hover(makeNavWhite, makeNavTransparent);
 		$sports.hover(makeDriveInactive, makeDriveActive);
 		$cards.children().on('click', function() {
 			$('html, body').animate(
 				{
 					scrollTop: window.innerHeight,
 					duration: 600,
 					easing: 'swing'
 				})
 		});
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
 
 		equalizeHeights($cards.find('.tt-homepage__card__body'));
 		makeNavTransparent();
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeMenuSticky(scroll);
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeMenuSticky(scroll) {
 			if (scroll > 80) {
 				makeNavWhite();
 			} else if (scroll <= 80) {
 				makeNavTransparent();
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var cardTitleHeight = 80;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var imgBottom = $cat.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = imgBottom + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - imgBottom});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeNavWhite() {
 			$nav.removeClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeNavTransparent() {
 			var isPanelOpen = $panels.hasClass('in');
 			var isScrolledDown = window.scrollY > 80;
 			if (isPanelOpen || isScrolledDown) { return; }
 
 			$nav.addClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveActive() {
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveInactive() {
 			$drive.addClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function equalizeHeights($elements) {
 			var maxHeight = 0;
 			$elements.each(function(i, el) { maxHeight = Math.max(el.clientHeight, maxHeight) } );
 
 			$elements.height(maxHeight);
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 		$(window).on('resize', onScroll);
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var menuHeight = 80;
 			var cardTitleHeight = 60;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var categoriesHeight = $drive.height() + $sports.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = categoriesHeight + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight - menuHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - categoriesHeight});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile and desktop
 	onReady(function() {
 		var time = 0.3;
 		var ease = Quad.easeOut;
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $sportsSubcats = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $driveSubcats = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $sportsSubcatItems = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $driveSubcatItems = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $sportsButton = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 		var $driveButton = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 
 		addEventListeners();
 
 		function addEventListeners() {
 			$sports.on('click', onClickSports);
 			$drive.on('click', onClickDrive);
 			$sportsSubcatItems.on('click', onClickSportsSubcatItem);
 			$driveSubcatItems.on('click', onClickDriveSubcatItem);
 		}
 
 		function onClickSports() {
 			if($sportsSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close drive
 			TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickDrive(e) {
 			if($driveSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close sports
 			TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickSportsSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$sportsSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function onClickDriveSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$driveSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function resetAllSubcatItems() {
 			TweenLite.set($sportsButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 	})
    </script>

 	.tt-main-navigation-module--transparent .tt-nav-right { display: none; }

 		font-size: 18px;
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="zh"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "微软雅黑體", "Microsoft YaHei", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ko"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Nanum Barun Gothic", "Malgun Gothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ja"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Hiragino Kaku Gothic Pro", "Meiryo", "Osaka", "MS PGothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	.tt-homepage__card__body {
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 		transition: height 200ms;
 	}

    <script>
     /* Detect if back-forward caching is used.
 	   This caused issues in Safari, where only the clicked subcat would stay visible after hitting back. */
 	window.addEventListener('unload', function () {});
 	window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
 		if (event.persisted) {
 			resetAllSubcatItems()
 		}
 	});
 
 
 	function onReady(method) {
 		if (window.jQuery) {
 			method();
 		} else {
 			setTimeout(function() { onReady(method) }, 50);
 		}
 	}
 
 	// Desktop only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (!isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 
 		var $nav = $('.tt-main-navigation-module');
 		var $cat = $('.tt-homepage__cat');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 		var $panels = $('.tt-panels');
 		var $logoImg = $nav.find('.tt-logo img');
 
 		$logoImg.get(0).onload = null; // Can be removed when TRIDUP-5616 is implemented.
 
 		$nav.hover(makeNavWhite, makeNavTransparent);
 		$sports.hover(makeDriveInactive, makeDriveActive);
 		$cards.children().on('click', function() {
 			$('html, body').animate(
 				{
 					scrollTop: window.innerHeight,
 					duration: 600,
 					easing: 'swing'
 				})
 		});
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
 
 		equalizeHeights($cards.find('.tt-homepage__card__body'));
 		makeNavTransparent();
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeMenuSticky(scroll);
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeMenuSticky(scroll) {
 			if (scroll > 80) {
 				makeNavWhite();
 			} else if (scroll <= 80) {
 				makeNavTransparent();
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var cardTitleHeight = 80;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var imgBottom = $cat.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = imgBottom + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - imgBottom});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeNavWhite() {
 			$nav.removeClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeNavTransparent() {
 			var isPanelOpen = $panels.hasClass('in');
 			var isScrolledDown = window.scrollY > 80;
 			if (isPanelOpen || isScrolledDown) { return; }
 
 			$nav.addClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveActive() {
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveInactive() {
 			$drive.addClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function equalizeHeights($elements) {
 			var maxHeight = 0;
 			$elements.each(function(i, el) { maxHeight = Math.max(el.clientHeight, maxHeight) } );
 
 			$elements.height(maxHeight);
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 		$(window).on('resize', onScroll);
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var menuHeight = 80;
 			var cardTitleHeight = 60;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var categoriesHeight = $drive.height() + $sports.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = categoriesHeight + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight - menuHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - categoriesHeight});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile and desktop
 	onReady(function() {
 		var time = 0.3;
 		var ease = Quad.easeOut;
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $sportsSubcats = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $driveSubcats = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $sportsSubcatItems = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $driveSubcatItems = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $sportsButton = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 		var $driveButton = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 
 		addEventListeners();
 
 		function addEventListeners() {
 			$sports.on('click', onClickSports);
 			$drive.on('click', onClickDrive);
 			$sportsSubcatItems.on('click', onClickSportsSubcatItem);
 			$driveSubcatItems.on('click', onClickDriveSubcatItem);
 		}
 
 		function onClickSports() {
 			if($sportsSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close drive
 			TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickDrive(e) {
 			if($driveSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close sports
 			TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickSportsSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$sportsSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function onClickDriveSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$driveSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function resetAllSubcatItems() {
 			TweenLite.set($sportsButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 	})
    </script>

 	.tt-main-navigation-module--transparent .tt-nav-right { display: none; }

 		font-size: 18px;
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="zh"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "微软雅黑體", "Microsoft YaHei", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ko"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Nanum Barun Gothic", "Malgun Gothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ja"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Hiragino Kaku Gothic Pro", "Meiryo", "Osaka", "MS PGothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	.tt-homepage__card__body {
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 		transition: height 200ms;
 	}

    <script>
     /* Detect if back-forward caching is used.
 	   This caused issues in Safari, where only the clicked subcat would stay visible after hitting back. */
 	window.addEventListener('unload', function () {});
 	window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
 		if (event.persisted) {
 			resetAllSubcatItems()
 		}
 	});
 
 
 	function onReady(method) {
 		if (window.jQuery) {
 			method();
 		} else {
 			setTimeout(function() { onReady(method) }, 50);
 		}
 	}
 
 	// Desktop only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (!isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 
 		var $nav = $('.tt-main-navigation-module');
 		var $cat = $('.tt-homepage__cat');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 		var $panels = $('.tt-panels');
 		var $logoImg = $nav.find('.tt-logo img');
 
 		$logoImg.get(0).onload = null; // Can be removed when TRIDUP-5616 is implemented.
 
 		$nav.hover(makeNavWhite, makeNavTransparent);
 		$sports.hover(makeDriveInactive, makeDriveActive);
 		$cards.children().on('click', function() {
 			$('html, body').animate(
 				{
 					scrollTop: window.innerHeight,
 					duration: 600,
 					easing: 'swing'
 				})
 		});
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
 
 		equalizeHeights($cards.find('.tt-homepage__card__body'));
 		makeNavTransparent();
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeMenuSticky(scroll);
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeMenuSticky(scroll) {
 			if (scroll > 80) {
 				makeNavWhite();
 			} else if (scroll <= 80) {
 				makeNavTransparent();
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var cardTitleHeight = 80;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var imgBottom = $cat.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = imgBottom + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - imgBottom});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeNavWhite() {
 			$nav.removeClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeNavTransparent() {
 			var isPanelOpen = $panels.hasClass('in');
 			var isScrolledDown = window.scrollY > 80;
 			if (isPanelOpen || isScrolledDown) { return; }
 
 			$nav.addClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveActive() {
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveInactive() {
 			$drive.addClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function equalizeHeights($elements) {
 			var maxHeight = 0;
 			$elements.each(function(i, el) { maxHeight = Math.max(el.clientHeight, maxHeight) } );
 
 			$elements.height(maxHeight);
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 		$(window).on('resize', onScroll);
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var menuHeight = 80;
 			var cardTitleHeight = 60;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var categoriesHeight = $drive.height() + $sports.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = categoriesHeight + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight - menuHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - categoriesHeight});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile and desktop
 	onReady(function() {
 		var time = 0.3;
 		var ease = Quad.easeOut;
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $sportsSubcats = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $driveSubcats = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $sportsSubcatItems = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $driveSubcatItems = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $sportsButton = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 		var $driveButton = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 
 		addEventListeners();
 
 		function addEventListeners() {
 			$sports.on('click', onClickSports);
 			$drive.on('click', onClickDrive);
 			$sportsSubcatItems.on('click', onClickSportsSubcatItem);
 			$driveSubcatItems.on('click', onClickDriveSubcatItem);
 		}
 
 		function onClickSports() {
 			if($sportsSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close drive
 			TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickDrive(e) {
 			if($driveSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close sports
 			TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickSportsSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$sportsSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function onClickDriveSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$driveSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function resetAllSubcatItems() {
 			TweenLite.set($sportsButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 	})
    </script>

 	.tt-main-navigation-module--transparent .tt-nav-right { display: none; }

 		font-size: 18px;
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="zh"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "微软雅黑體", "Microsoft YaHei", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ko"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Nanum Barun Gothic", "Malgun Gothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	html[lang="ja"] .tt-homepage__card__title {
 		font-family: "Gotham SSM Medium", "Hiragino Kaku Gothic Pro", "Meiryo", "Osaka", "MS PGothic", "Arial Unicode MS", "Helvetica Neue", Helvetica, sans-serif;
 	}
 
 	.tt-homepage__card__body {
 		margin-bottom: 20px;
 		transition: height 200ms;
 	}

    <script>
     /* Detect if back-forward caching is used.
 	   This caused issues in Safari, where only the clicked subcat would stay visible after hitting back. */
 	window.addEventListener('unload', function () {});
 	window.addEventListener('pageshow', function(event) {
 		if (event.persisted) {
 			resetAllSubcatItems()
 		}
 	});
 
 
 	function onReady(method) {
 		if (window.jQuery) {
 			method();
 		} else {
 			setTimeout(function() { onReady(method) }, 50);
 		}
 	}
 
 	// Desktop only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (!isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 
 		var $nav = $('.tt-main-navigation-module');
 		var $cat = $('.tt-homepage__cat');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 		var $panels = $('.tt-panels');
 		var $logoImg = $nav.find('.tt-logo img');
 
 		$logoImg.get(0).onload = null; // Can be removed when TRIDUP-5616 is implemented.
 
 		$nav.hover(makeNavWhite, makeNavTransparent);
 		$sports.hover(makeDriveInactive, makeDriveActive);
 		$cards.children().on('click', function() {
 			$('html, body').animate(
 				{
 					scrollTop: window.innerHeight,
 					duration: 600,
 					easing: 'swing'
 				})
 		});
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 
 
 		equalizeHeights($cards.find('.tt-homepage__card__body'));
 		makeNavTransparent();
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeMenuSticky(scroll);
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeMenuSticky(scroll) {
 			if (scroll > 80) {
 				makeNavWhite();
 			} else if (scroll <= 80) {
 				makeNavTransparent();
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var cardTitleHeight = 80;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var imgBottom = $cat.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = imgBottom + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - imgBottom});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 
 		function makeNavWhite() {
 			$nav.removeClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeNavTransparent() {
 			var isPanelOpen = $panels.hasClass('in');
 			var isScrolledDown = window.scrollY > 80;
 			if (isPanelOpen || isScrolledDown) { return; }
 
 			$nav.addClass('tt-main-navigation-module--transparent');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveActive() {
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function makeDriveInactive() {
 			$drive.addClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 
 		function equalizeHeights($elements) {
 			var maxHeight = 0;
 			$elements.each(function(i, el) { maxHeight = Math.max(el.clientHeight, maxHeight) } );
 
 			$elements.height(maxHeight);
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile only
 	onReady(function() {
 		var isDesktop = window.innerWidth >= 1024;
 		if (isDesktop) {
 			return;
 		}
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $cards = $('.tt-homepage__cards');
 
 		$(window).on('scroll', onScroll);
 		$(window).on('resize', onScroll);
 		onScroll();
 
 		function onScroll() {
 			var scroll = window.scrollY;
 
 			makeCardsSticky(scroll)
 		}
 
 		function makeCardsSticky(scroll) {
 			var menuHeight = 80;
 			var cardTitleHeight = 60;
 			var cardDefaultTop = -20;
 			var categoriesHeight = $drive.height() + $sports.height();
 			var cardDefaultPos = categoriesHeight + cardDefaultTop;
 			var winHeight = window.innerHeight - menuHeight;
 			var theFold = scroll + winHeight;
 			var theCutoff = theFold - cardTitleHeight;
 
 			if (cardDefaultPos > theCutoff) {
 				$cards.css({top: theCutoff - categoriesHeight});
 			} else {
 				$cards.attr('style', '');
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	// Mobile and desktop
 	onReady(function() {
 		var time = 0.3;
 		var ease = Quad.easeOut;
 
 		var $sports = $('.tt-homepage__cat#sports');
 		var $drive = $('.tt-homepage__cat#drive');
 		var $sportsSubcats = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $driveSubcats = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcats');
 		var $sportsSubcatItems = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $driveSubcatItems = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__subcat');
 		var $sportsButton = $sports.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 		var $driveButton = $drive.find('.tt-homepage__button');
 
 		addEventListeners();
 
 		function addEventListeners() {
 			$sports.on('click', onClickSports);
 			$drive.on('click', onClickDrive);
 			$sportsSubcatItems.on('click', onClickSportsSubcatItem);
 			$driveSubcatItems.on('click', onClickDriveSubcatItem);
 		}
 
 		function onClickSports() {
 			if($sportsSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close drive
 			TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickDrive(e) {
 			if($driveSubcats.css('opacity') < 1) {
 				var subcatOffset = '-50';
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '-50', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: subcatOffset, ease: ease });
 			} else {
 				TweenLite.to($driveButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 				TweenLite.to($driveSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			}
 			// Also close sports
 			TweenLite.to($sportsButton, time, { autoAlpha: 1, y: '0', ease: ease });
 			TweenLite.to($sportsSubcats, time, { autoAlpha: 0, y: '0', ease: ease });
 		}
 
 		function onClickSportsSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$sportsSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function onClickDriveSubcatItem(e) {
 			/*$driveSubcatItems.each(function(i, el) {
 				if(el !== e.currentTarget) {
 					TweenLite.to(this, 1, { autoAlpha: 0, ease: ease });
 				}
 			})*/
 
 			e.stopPropagation();
 		}
 
 		function resetAllSubcatItems() {
 			TweenLite.set($sportsButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveButton, { autoAlpha: 1, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcats, { autoAlpha: 0, y: 0 });
 			TweenLite.set($sportsSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			TweenLite.set($driveSubcatItems, { autoAlpha: 1 });
 			$drive.removeClass('tt-homepage__cat--inactive');
 		}
 	})
    </script>

 	.tt-main-navigation-module--transparent .tt-nav-right { display: none; }
